 On July 23, the Supreme Court had asked the state government to suggest a name for appointment to the post of Lokayukta till August 22, after which the government decided the name of Ravindra Singh Yadav and sent the file related to it to Raj Bhavan for the first time on August 5
 tippaniyan After the formation of Akhilesh Yadav government in the state in March 2012, it was said that the Lokayukta's tenure in the state should be increased from six to eight years
 maujuuda lokayukta enke mehrotra nau saal se is pad par hai
 While sending the file back, the Governor made it clear that the Chief Minister, Chief Justice of Allahabad High Court and the Leader of the State Legislative Assembly will give their approval on the file only after the name is decided in the meeting of the selection committee of the opposition
 rajyapal nik ne bataaya ki sarkaar ne shanivaar ko chauthi baar bheji file main pun: avkaash praapt nyaayamurti rabindra singh yadav ke niyukti kii sifarish kii he
 He said that the government has said that there is a two-member selection committee of the Chief Minister and the Leader of Opposition for appointment to this post and both have met in this regard
 rajyapal ne kaha ki mukhyamantri akhilesh kii taraf se ai file main kaha gaya he ki lokayukta kii niyukti ke bare main ucch nyaayalay ke mukhya nyaayadhish kii bhi salaah le lee gai he
 But it is not binding on the selection process
 nik ne kaha ki vah sarkaar kii sifarish ke vibhinn pahaluon par nyaayik raay le rahe hai or jo bhi nirnay hoga sheeghra hi le lenge
 Leader of Opposition Swami Prasad Maurya says that the Chief Justice is also a member in the selection committee and the consent of all three is required for the recommendation of any one name
 maury ne kaha, ‘‘mujhase hui charchaa main mukhyamantri ne kaha ki is sambandh main elahabaad ucch nyaayalay ke mukhya nyaayadhish nyaayamurti di vaai chandrachud se bhi vichaar-vimarsh ho chukaa he or unhone apni sanstuti pradaan kar di he
 '' unhone kaha ki is sambandh main 5-6 baithken hui, magar kisi main bhi mukhya nyaayadhish shaamil nahin the
 On August 21, the Governor sent back the files related to the appointment of the Lokayukta to the government for the third time, saying that in view of the Supreme Court's order passed on July 23, the Chief Justice of the Chief Minister of Allahabad High Court and the Leader of the State Legislative Assembly, the opposition consulted and After concurrence, propose one name for appointment of new Lokayukta
 nik ne file teesri baar lautaate hue 10 prishthon kaa patr likhaa tha, jisamen unhone mukhya nyaayadhish chandrachud ke patron kaa zikr kiya tha, jisamen unhone kaha tha, ‘‘chaar main se teen patron main maine nyaayamurti rabindra singh kii niyukti se asahmat hone ke kaaran bataaye the
 i want to clarify those reasons by reiterating that i do not agree with the appointment of Ravindra Singh to the post of Lokayukta
 ’’ The Governor referred to another letter from Justice Chandrachud, in which he mentioned the presence of Justice Ravindra Singh along with senior government minister Shivpal Singh Yadav at a public function, in the public eye towards a particular party
 There is a doubt that the person having an inclination will be able to execute the responsibility of the Lokayukta in a fair manner
 ucchtam nyaayalay ne gat 23 july ko rajya sarkaar se kaha tha ki vah lokayukta pad par niyukti ke liye 22 agast tak koi naam sujhaaye jiske baad sarkaar ne rabindra singh yadav kaa naam tay karke usase sambandhit file paanch agast ko pehali baar rajbhavan ko bheji thi
 The comments pradesh main march 2012 main akhilesh yadav sarkaar ke gathan ke baad pradesh main lokayukta ke kaarykaal ko chah se badhaakar aath saal karne kii baat kahi gai thi
 The current Lokayukta NK Mehrotra has been in this position for nine years

 Air India suspended its Regional Director (eastern Region) Rohit Bhasin for allegedly stealing a wallet from a tax-free shop at Sydney Airport
 bhasin ke bina anumati ke air india parisar main pravesh karne par bhi roak laga di gai he
 The officials gave this information on Sunday
 parisar main pravesh karne par roak lagane ke alaava unhen apana pahchaan patr jamaa karaane kaa bhi nirdesh diya gaya he
 Rohit Bhasin was posted as a commander (pilot) of the AI 301 aircraft
 unka vimaan 22 june kii subah 10
 45 am (local time) to leave for Sydney from Delhi airport
 airline ke ek pravaktaa ne kaha, 'praarambhik report ke mutabik ek captain mistar rohit bhasin sidney main ek kar mukt dukaan se wolet chori karte pakade gaye
 Bhasin is also the Regional Director
 air india ne is ghatana kii jaanch shuru kar di he or tab tak captain ko nilambit kar diya gaya he
 The suspension order issued on Saturday by the airline stated, 'according to the report given by the regional manager of Australia, you allegedly stolen goods from a duty free shop at Sydney Airport before the departure of flight AI 301 on 22 June 2019
 Has acted aapke khilaaf kisi bhi anushaasanamak karrwai ke shuru karne or jaanch puri hone tak aapako tatkaal prabhaav se nilambit kiya jaataa he
 ' seychelles ke raashtrapati danni for apane pehle bharat daure par hai

 Narendra Batra says that barring a few corporate houses, others do lip service
 in games ke liye zyada corporate aage nahin aate
 The state government and the corporate world should come forward
 jabaki hockey patrkaar ke armugam in sabase liye hockey tantra ko zimmedaar maanate hai
 He says that if you do one or two tournaments in a year, how will the corporate help you
 aapako indian badminton lig kii tarah kuch alag kuch nayaa karnaa hoga
 You will be able to help you only when you think for the corporate world
 tippaniyan Amidst all this, coach Narendra Singh Saini or the coach of the women's team, MK Kaushik, says so much that the team has good junior players and if they take advantage of this opportunity, then the hockey building can be erected
 hockey kii jeet or unke swaagat samaaroh ke liye chaar din kii chandani vaali kahawat kaa istemaal karnaa shaayad jyaadati ho lekin hockey tantra or corporate jagat ne iskaa istamaal sahi tareeke se nahin kiya to is jeet kii ahmiyat bhi sirf itihaas ban sakati he
 This has been happening continuously
 junior world cap main aitihaasik jeet ke baad hockey khilaadiyon ko ek−ek lakh rupee kii inami raqam di gai jabaki sabhi saport staff ke sadasyon ko pachaas−pachaas hazaar rupee kii raqam di gai
 Although this amount is not big, but the players do not even regret it
 lekin fikr is baat kii he ki is team ke aane vaale kal kii tasviir bahut saafe nahin
 The sponsors and job hunt are on for most players
 in junior khilaadiyon ne hockey ke maidan par itihaas kaayam kar apni zimmedaari nibhaa di he
 Hockey India is impressed by the actions of all these players and support staff, but it is not in their hands to pay more than this
 corporate jagat filhal is jeet kii gunj nahin sun paa rahaa or bekabar hone kaa swang rach rahaa he
 It can be worse if you listen to the condition and need of the players
 ranchi kii super hero golkeeper bigan soy kahati hai 'jo bhi paisa mila he use ghar banane main kharch karuungi
 The entire house will not be built with this, but will do
 main bahut khush hum
 ' railway main kaam karne vaali vandana kataaria kii haalat bigan soy se behatar he
 His father has a job in the public sector
 vandana kahati hai, 'ye paise main gharavaalon ko de duungi
 They need unke kaam aegi
 
 
 But he hopes that with this victory, the corporate world and sponsors will surely come forward to help him
 pehle bhi apane liye alag prerana talashkar maidan par karnama karne vaali in ladakiyon kaa hausala tutaa nahin he
 They all play with the hope that the picture of hockey will change one day
 world cap main player of da toornament baniin rani rampal kahati hai
 
 
 'I think this picture will definitely change
 ye tasviir badalani chahie
 ' karnataka kii emen punamma ke paas koi naukari nahin he lekin vah hockey kii dasha or uski vajah ko samajhati hai
 She says, 'this is the first step
 abhi aane vaale toornament main ham or mehnat karengi

 The ongoing development work in Chhattisgarh has been severely hurt by the Naxalites
 chhattisgarh ke bastar zile main naksaliyon ne road nirmaan ke kaary ko thapp kar diya 
 The target of completing the construction work before the rains in these areas was set two years ago
 lakshya ko puraa karne ke liye police or kendriya suraksha balon ne apni puri takat jhok bhi di thi
 But due to major Naxalite attacks, the government's aspirations have been destroyed
 nirmaan kaary kii raftaar ko rokane main naksaliyon ne kamyaabi hasil kar lee he
 Neither workers nor government officials, contractors and security personnel are seen in more than two dozen roads in Bastar
 darasal tamaam sadakon se police or kendriya suraksha balon ko hataa liya gaya he
 Due to this, construction work has stopped there
 sukama hamale ke baad se CRPF sadake chhod laut gai apane barracksukama ke burkapal main CRPF javaanon par hue hamale ke baad bastar kii 25 sadakon kaa nirmaan aadhe main latak gaya he 
 Work on these roads has been stopped for 6 months
 maovadi hamale kii ashanka ke chalate bastar ke sabhi saat zilon main thekedaar or majdoor bhi sadak nirmaan sthalon se apana saamaan samet kar ja chuke he
 No roads were built in these areas since independence
 purvi madhyapradesh ke jamaane main zyaadaatar ilaakon main sirf kachi sadake bani thi
 | These roads were also repaired rarely
 2001 menchhattisgarhrajya ke gathan ke baad bhi yahi haal rahaa
 The condition of these roads remained the same even during the ten years of the first Congress and then the tenure of Chief Minister Raman Singh
 kyoki in ilaake main naksali puri tarah se haaavee rahe hai
 When the BJP came to power for the third time, the construction works in Bastar started gaining momentum
 khaastaur par naksal prabhavit ilaakon main police houseing corporation ne sadak nirmaan kaary kii jimmedaari apane kandho main lee jisase gaanv kii tasviir badalane lagi
 Instead of the forest paths, the villagers started walking on paved roads
 gaanv main awajahi bhi shuru ho gai
 Passenger bus, jeep, car and other vehicles also started moving
 saath hi saath police or suraksha balon ke vaahan bhi in sadakon par daudane lage
 This is what the Naxalites started thinking about
 police or suraksha balon ke vaahan unki aakhon kii kirakiri ban gayi
 The Maoists, freshly minted, villagers, started targeting the CRPF team engaged in security of road construction instead of the common force
 isi saal pehle sukama main 11 march ko CRPF ke daste par hamalaa kar 11 javaanon ko nishaanaa banaaya
 After this, on 24 April, 25 CRPF personnel were martyred in Naxalite attack in Sukma
 donon ghatnaon se rajya or centre kii sarkaar sakate main aa gai
 After the attack in Sukamake Burukapal, then CRPF DGP 'sudhir Lakhtakiya' had instructed not to build the road and move the force
 jiske baad force apane baiyrakon main laut gai
 Since then, the entire road construction work has been stalled in many areas
 yah kaam kab shuru hoga iske bare main naa to chhattisgarh police kuch kah paa rahi he or naa hi CRPF 
 The construction of the road had raised hopes of the people of the area that it was late but the government took care of them
 maovadiyon ne ek baar phir graminon ke vikaas ke sapanom par pani pher diya he
 BJP will start campaigning in Bihar from today
 rajdhani patna main party adhyaksh amit shah ke saath bijepi ke kai bade netaa maujuud rahenge
 BJP general secretary and in-charge of Bihar affairs Bhupendra Yadav said that these chariots will visit 10 villages every day and will reach the public through audio and video publicity materials of the party
 bataaya ja rahaa he ki is kaarykram main endie ke sahyogi dalon ke netaa bhi shaamil honge

 party ke sachiv shrikant sharma ne bataaya ki rajg kaa prachaar abhiyaan ‘‘garib samarthak narendra modi sarkaar kii muhim or bhaajapa se naata todane ke baad nitish sarkaar ke kushasan’’ ke dohare sandesh par aadhaarit hoga

 unke ye nijee byore tab achaanak logon kii najar main aae, jab unhone paaya ki unka naam 31 agast ko prakashit rashtriya naagarikta register (enarasi) main nahin he
 This register was prepared to identify illegal intruders in the state
 aisa isliye karnaa padaa kyonki puure rajya main virodh pradarshan hue or aarope lagaae gaye the ki assam ke maidani ilaakon main bangladesh se avaidh ghuspaithiyon kii baadh aa gai he
 a total of 3,30,27,661 people residing within the geographical boundary of Assam had applied for their names in the register, out of which 19,06,657 have been left out
 to enarasi main naam shaamil nahin hone kaa matlab kya yah he ki maalo bharat ke naagarik nahin hai? kya maalo vidhansabha kii apni sadsyta ganvaa baithenge? kya ve apni jameen kii milkiyat ganvaa denge? kya ve dobaaraa vot de paaenge? kya unhen giraftaar kiya jayega yaa ditension camp yaa bandi shivi main rakhaa jayega or phir aakhirkaar us desh main waapas bhej diya jayega jahaan se ve kathith taur par aae hai?maalo ke saath aisa kuch nahin hoga or un 19 lakh se zyada duusare logon ke saath bhi nahin, jinke naam enarasi main nahin aae hai
 They will continue to get all the rights and facilities from the Government of India as before
 aisa isliye ki abhi do or paaydaan baaki hai
 Since the Supreme Court has been directly monitoring the process of updating the NRC since 2015, it must first approve the list published by the state coordinator of the NRC
 adaalat ise puraa kaa puraa manjuur yaa naamanzoor kar sakati he yaa thode herpher ke saath bhi manjuur kar sakati he
 The Registrar General of India (RGI) will have to notify it after the court approves it, as the Government of India is the sole custodian in the matter of citizenship
 lihaaja 31 agast ko prakashit suchi keval usee din se lagu hogi jab isaki gajet adhisuchana jari kar di jaaegi
 Those left out will then be able to appeal against the expulsion of their names to the Foreign Tribunal or Arbitration (FT) and for this they will get four months from the date of notification
 ye panchat logon kii naagarikta ke darje par faisla dene ke liye hi banaae gaye hai
